<time>1547098874420<//time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
Good library for the most part. Lots of books. Lots of computers. Summer meal programs for children in need and even a seed exchange to encourage gardening. Staff is very helpful.  The only problems I've seen are just a result of lack of funding. Some of the books are rather old and could use replacing. Occasionally I come across a series with one or two books missing. All in all, For downtown Stockton they're doing pretty good.</review>

<review>I hired this company to do flooring, paver patio, retaining wall, artificial grass, and rocks

They hire subcontractors to do all the work... save yourself the money and look for local contractors or go directly to suppliers instead of going through 1StopBuilder... you are better off hiring Homedepot or Lowes... shop around

They increase cost from the start and then offer so many 'deals/discounts' Don't fall for it.. Nothing but hot air! Yelp review discount, doing a video discount, or finance discount... all joke!

They purposely do not include everything in writing with the contract. Later when you remind them, they deny the whole agreement saying 'we never do this for our clients, I don't know why I would promise you this'

I wouldn't recommend this company to anybody. They use ill practices, will manipulate you the second they find an opportunity, and if you happen to cancel a part of the project because of their failure... then you can consider throwing money down the drain! They won't own up to their mistakes, instead you end up paying for it, literally paying for it!

Even after getting paid in full, they send people to my house without my permission, trespassing in my property, because they want '100% completion document signed' or else they won't release warranty..

At the end...
They never gave solar lights for my backyard as promised ...
Baseboard installation with the new floor was poorly done...
My retaining wall was not installed to contractual measure by a whole layer of blocks and they never adjusted my contract to reduce cost...

<user_id>104733637577864323292< /user_id><gmapID>0x80c286c022a59729:0xef52b1cbc0915b74< /gmapID>< Review>
We took our dog here last week and loved the way he looked after. He was very clean and his nails were cut so well for a good price! Two days later, he started yelping in pain whenever we pet his back or neck. We took him to the vet yesterday concerned about his back, and the vet discovered infected scabs (blood and pus) all down his spine and neck. The vet told us she sees this from groomers who comb too rigorously (leaving cuts in the skin) and do not sanitize their brushes, which leaves bacteria to infect the cuts. We paid a $100 vet bill and got him started on antibiotics. This is incredibly disappointing as it was our first experience with this groomer, and will definitely be the last. Please sanitize your brushes!</Review>

<username>Wes Lambert<//username><Time>1472520558833< /Time><Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Best Denny's in Santa Clara

I've frequented many Denny's restaurants throughout the US, and this one is my new favorite.   The Service is Excellent, the Food is Excellent and the price is usually the same wherever you go (but still good).

I often get the Pot Roast and I can say that it has been a long time since I've considered ordering it again in the same sitting (to go).

Denny's always has great down-home favorites such as Pot Roast,  Country-Fried Steak, Spaghetti and Meatballs,  or Fish and Chips.  This restaurant does them all a service.

If you want a good idea of how amazing Denny's can be, eat at this location.</Review>
